<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem6.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f:G\to H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math> is a homomorphism, then the <em class="ltx_emph ltx_font_upright">kernal</em> <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem6.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathop{ker}f=\left\{{g\in G\mid f(g)=e}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>e</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mi>f</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>e</mi></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math>, and the <em class="ltx_emph ltx_font_upright">image</em> <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem6.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathop{im}f=\left\{{f(g)\mid g\in G}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow><mi>f</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math> are subgroups of <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem6.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> and <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem6.p1.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H" display="inline"><mi>H</mi></math> respectively.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem7" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.2.7</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem7.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem7.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g:G\to H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math> homomorphism, then <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem7.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathop{ker}f\triangleleft G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>e</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mi>f</mi></mrow><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.p5" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">For any <math id="Ch1.Sx1.p5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k\in\mathop{ker}f" display="inline"><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>e</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mi>f</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, for any <math id="Ch1.Sx1.p5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g\in G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.Sx1.p5.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f(gkg^{-1})=f(g)f(k)f(g)^{-1}=f(g)f(g)^{-1}=e" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>e</mi></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch1.Sx1.p5.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="gkg^{-1}\in\ker f" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi>ker</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mi>f</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<section id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1" class="ltx_subsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">1.2.1 </span>Isomorphism Theorems</h4>

<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">We describe common cases for when groups are isomorphic, as summarized by the three isomorphism theorems.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem8" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.2.8</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem8.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem8.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f:G\to H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math> is surjective homomorphism, then for <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem8.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="K=\ker f" display="inline"><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>ker</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mi>f</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem8.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G/K\cong H" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>≅</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Consider the map <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi:G/K\to H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math> sending <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="gK\to f(g)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.</p>
<ul id="Ch1.Sx1.I3" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">If <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i1.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g_{1}K=g_{2}K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i1.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g_{1}=g_{2}k" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, and <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i1.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi(g_{1}K)=f(g_{1})=f(g_{2}k)=f(g_{2})f(k)=f(g_{2})=\pi(g_{2}K)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>k</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">For <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i2.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g_{1}K,g_{2}K\in G/K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i2.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi((g_{1}K)(g_{2})K)=\pi((g_{1}g_{2})K)=f(g_{1}g_{2})=f(g_{1})f(g_{2})=\pi(g_%
{1}K)\pi(g_{2}K)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i3" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">For any <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i3.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="h\in H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i3.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="h=f(g)" display="inline"><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i3.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi(gK)=f(g)=h" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>h</mi></mrow></math></p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i4" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">If <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i4.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi(g_{1}K)=\pi(g_{2}K)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i4.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f(g_{1})=f(g_{2})" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i4.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g_{1}g_{2}^{-1}=k" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msubsup><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow></math>, and <math id="Ch1.Sx1.I3.i4.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g_{1}K=g_{2}K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>g</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="ltx_p">∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem9" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.2.9</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem9.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem9.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H&lt;G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem9.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\triangleleft G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem9.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H/(H\cap N)=(HN)/N" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>∩</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem9.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="HN=\left\{{hn\mid h\in H,n\in n}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Indeed <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="HN&lt;G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, with <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(h_{1}n_{1})(h_{2}n_{2})^{-1}=h_{1}n_{1}n_{2}^{-1}h_{2}=\overbrace{(h_{1}h_{2}%
)}^{\text{in }H}\overbrace{\left(h_{2}^{-1}(n_{1}n_{2}^{-1})h_{2}\right)}^{%
\text{in }N}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msubsup><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msubsup><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mover><mover accent="true"><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏞</mo></mover><mrow><mtext>in </mtext><mo>⁢</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mover><mo>⁢</mo><mover><mover accent="true"><mrow><mo>(</mo><mrow><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msubsup><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msubsup><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo>)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="true">⏞</mo></mover><mrow><mtext>in </mtext><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mover></mrow></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p4" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Additionally, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\triangleleft HN" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, since for any <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="h\in HN" display="inline"><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="hnh^{-1}\in N" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Finally, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H\cap N\triangleleft H" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>∩</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math>, since for any <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="h\in H,n\in H\cap N" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>∩</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="hnh^{-1}\in N" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></math> (normality of <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline"><mi>N</mi></math>) and <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="hnh^{-1}\in H" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math> (closure of <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p5.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H" display="inline"><mi>H</mi></math>).</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p6" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Thus, consider the surjective homomorphism <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi:H\to(HN)/N" display="inline"><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></mrow></math> sending <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="h\to(he)N=hN" display="inline"><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>e</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p6.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="K=\mathop{ker}\pi=H\cap N" display="inline"><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>e</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>r</mi></mrow><mi>π</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>∩</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
Thus, applying the first isomorphism theorem, we obtain the result.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem10" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.2.10</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem10.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem10.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H,N\triangleleft G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>,</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, with <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem10.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N&lt;H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math>.
Then, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem10.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(G/N)/(H/N)\cong G/H" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>≅</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p7" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Indeed, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p7.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H/N\triangleleft G/N" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, since <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p7.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(gN)(hN)(g^{-1}N)=(ghg^{-1})N=h_{1}N\in H/N" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
Thus, considering the surjective map <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p7.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi:G/N\to H/N" display="inline"><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow></mrow></math> sending <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p7.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="gN\to gH" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, with <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS1.p7.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="K=\ker\pi=\left\{{gK\mid gH=H}\right\}=H/K" display="inline"><mrow><mi>K</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>ker</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mi>π</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
Thus, applying the first isomorphism theorem, we obtain the result.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2" class="ltx_subsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">1.2.2 </span>Generators and Representations</h4>

<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">In addition to applying isomorphism theorems, we can study the generators of a group.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem11" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_definition">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Definition 1.2.11</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem11.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem11.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S\subset G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>⊂</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, then the group generated by <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem11.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline"><mi>S</mi></math>, <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem11.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\langle S\rangle=\bigcap_{S\subset H&lt;G}H" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><msub><mo>⋂</mo><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>⊂</mo><mi>H</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></msub><mi>H</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, is the smallest subgroup containing <math id="Ch1.Sx1.Thmtheorem11.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline"><mi>S</mi></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">For example, considering the dihedral group <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2.p2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="D_{n}" display="inline"><msub><mi>D</mi><mi>n</mi></msub></math>, the generators are <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2.p2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\rho" display="inline"><mi>ρ</mi></math> and <math id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2.p2.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\tau" display="inline"><mi>τ</mi></math>
// TODO</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.Sx1.SS2.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Moreover, an important way homomorphisms are applied is to change the study of groups to the study of linear transformations.
For example, the sign function.
// TODO</p>
</div>
</section>
</section>
<section id="Ch1.S3" class="ltx_section">
<h3 class="ltx_title ltx_title_section">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_section">1.3 </span>Classification of Groups</h3>

<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_example">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Example 1.3.1</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Consider a group <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> of order <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p" display="inline"><mi>p</mi></math>, where <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p" display="inline"><mi>p</mi></math> is prime.
Then, for <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="e\neq g\in G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>e</mi><mo>≠</mo><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, then the subgroup <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\langle g\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></math> has order <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n\geq 2" display="inline"><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>≥</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow></math> (since <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="e,g\in\langle g\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>e</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></math>).
But, we know that since <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n\mid p" display="inline"><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>∣</mo><mi>p</mi></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n=p" display="inline"><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>p</mi></mrow></math>, and so <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem1.p1.m10" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G=\langle g\rangle\cong Z_{p}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo>≅</mo><msub><mi>Z</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Above, we classified groups of prime order by studying the subgroups of <math id="Ch1.S3.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math>.
To extend this idea, we will develop the Sylow theorems to understand important subgroups of <math id="Ch1.S3.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math>.
Then, we apply the isomorphism theorems to understand how these subgroups compose together to build up to <math id="Ch1.S3.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math>.</p>
</div>
<section id="Ch1.S3.SS1" class="ltx_subsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">1.3.1 </span>Sylow Theorems</h4>

<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">First, we describe the subgroups that we are looking for:</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_definition">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Definition 1.3.2</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{G}\right|=p^{n}m" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p\nmid m" display="inline"><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>∤</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow></math>.
Then, a <em class="ltx_emph ltx_font_upright">p-subgroup</em> <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H" display="inline"><mi>H</mi></math> has order <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p^{k}" display="inline"><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi></msup></math> for some <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k&gt;0" display="inline"><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math>.
Moreover, we say <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H" display="inline"><mi>H</mi></math> is a <em class="ltx_emph ltx_font_upright">p-Sylow</em> subogroup if <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k=n" display="inline"><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Towards this, we also consider the subgroup,</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem3" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_definition">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Definition 1.3.3</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">The <em class="ltx_emph ltx_font_upright">normalizer</em> <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N_{G}(H)=\left\{{g\in G\mid gHg^{-1}=H}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>N</mi><mi>G</mi></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>H</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>H</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>g</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Our main tool towards finding such subgroups is going to be through actions and fixed points (contrast: stabilizers).</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_definition">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Definition 1.3.4</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> acts on <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="x\in X" display="inline"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow></math> is a <em class="ltx_emph ltx_font_upright">fixed-point</em> when <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\forall g\in G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo rspace="0.167em">∀</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g\cdot x=x" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow></math>.
We denote <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem4.p1.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X^{G}" display="inline"><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>G</mi></msup></math> the fixed points.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem5" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_lemma">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Lemma 1.3.5</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem5.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem5.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> acts on <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem5.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem5.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{G}\right|=p^{k}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi></msup></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem5.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{X^{G}}\right|\equiv_{p}\left|{X}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>G</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Recall that the set of orbits partition <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math>.
Focusing on an orbit <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G\cdot x" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow></math>, we know that <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p^{k}=\left|{G}\right|=\left|{G/G_{x}}\right|\left|{G\cdot x}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi></msup><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>x</mi></msub></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.
Thus, for <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G_{x}\neq G" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>x</mi></msub><mo>≠</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math> (i.e. <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="x\not\in X^{G}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>∉</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>G</mi></msup></mrow></math>), <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p4.m6" class="ltx_math_unparsed" alttext="p\mid\left|{G\cdot x}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0.167em">∣</mo><mo fence="false" rspace="0.167em">|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>x</mi><mo fence="false">|</mo></mrow></math>.
So, collecting the fixed points and non-fixed points,</p>
<table id="Ch1.Ex3" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_center"><math id="Ch1.Ex3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{X}\right|=\left|{X^{G}}\right|+\sum_{x}(G\cdot x)\equiv_{p}\left|{X^{G}%
}\right|" display="block"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>G</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em">+</mo><mrow><munder><mo movablelimits="false" rspace="0em">∑</mo><mi>x</mi></munder><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>G</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p class="ltx_p">∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p5" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Now, we are ready to prove the Sylow theorems.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem6" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.3.6</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem6.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem6.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{G}\right|=p^{n}m" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow></mrow></math> for <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem6.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p\nmid m" display="inline"><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>∤</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem6.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> has a <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem6.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p" display="inline"><mi>p</mi></math>-Sylow subgroup.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p6" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">We prove via induction that for any <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="0&lt;k\leq n" display="inline"><mrow><mn>0</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></math>, that there is a subgroup of order <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p^{k}" display="inline"><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi></msup></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">For <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k=1" display="inline"><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></math>, consider <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X=\left\{{(a_{1},\ldots,a_{p})\in G^{p}\mid a_{1}\cdots a_{p}=e}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>G</mi><mi>p</mi></msup></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⋯</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>e</mi></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.
Then, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m3" class="ltx_math_unparsed" alttext="\left|\bigr{.}X\right|=\left|\bigr{.}G\right|^{p-1}" display="inline"><mrow><mo fence="false">|</mo><mo lspace="0.167em" mathsize="1.200em" rspace="0.167em">.</mo><mi>X</mi><mo fence="false">|</mo><mo lspace="0.167em" rspace="0em">=</mo><mo fence="false">|</mo><mo lspace="0.167em" mathsize="1.200em" rspace="0.167em">.</mo><mi>G</mi><msup><mo fence="false">|</mo><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></math>, since <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="a_{p}=(a_{1}\cdots a_{p-1})^{-1}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⋯</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></math> has <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p-1" display="inline"><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></math> degrees of freedom.
Consider <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f:X\to X" display="inline"><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow></mrow></math> sending <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(a_{1},\ldots,a_{p})\mapsto(a_{p},a_{1},\ldots,a_{p-1})" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math>, and the action <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathbb{Z}_{p}" display="inline"><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></math> on <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m10" class="ltx_Math" alttext="k\cdot x=f^{k}(x)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>x</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>f</mi><mi>k</mi></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.
We find a non-trivial fixed point of <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m11" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f" display="inline"><mi>f</mi></math> is an element <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m12" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(a,\ldots,a)" display="inline"><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m13" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{\langle a\rangle}\right|=p" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>p</mi></mrow></math>.
Indeed, for each of the <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m14" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N" display="inline"><mi>N</mi></math> non-fixed orbits, each having order exactly <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m15" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p" display="inline"><mi>p</mi></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m16" class="ltx_Math" alttext="0\equiv_{p}\left|{X}\right|\equiv_{p}\left|{X^{\mathbb{Z}_{p}}}\right|+pN%
\equiv_{p}\left|{X^{\mathbb{Z}_{p}}}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><mn>0</mn><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>N</mi></mrow></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.
Thus, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p7.m17" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{X^{\mathbb{Z}_{p}}}\right|\geq p" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>≥</mo><mi>p</mi></mrow></math> (non-empty).</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Otherwise, for <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1&lt;k\leq n" display="inline"><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>k</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></math>, suppose we have <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="K" display="inline"><mi>K</mi></math>, a subgroup of order <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p^{k-1}" display="inline"><msup><mi>p</mi><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></math>.
Then, consider the action <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="K" display="inline"><mi>K</mi></math> on <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G/K" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p\cdot(gK)\mapsto(ag)K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, and the normalizer <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N(K)/K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></math>.</p>
<ul id="Ch1.S3.I1" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="Ch1.S3.I1.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.S3.I1.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><math id="Ch1.S3.I1.i1.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N(K)/K\cong(G/K)^{K}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>≅</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mi>K</mi></msup></mrow></math>, since <math id="Ch1.S3.I1.i1.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="gK\in N(K)/K\iff\forall a\in K,ag=gk_{a}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⇔</mo><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo rspace="0.167em">∀</mo><mi>a</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>k</mi><mi>a</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, i.e. <math id="Ch1.S3.I1.i1.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="gK" display="inline"><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></math> is a fixed-point.</p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="Ch1.S3.I1.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.S3.I1.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><math id="Ch1.S3.I1.i2.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{N(K)/K}\right|=\left|{(G/K)^{K}}\right|\equiv_{p}\left|{G/K}\right|=p^{%
n-k+1}m\equiv_{p}0" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mi>K</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>p</mi><mrow><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>−</mo><mi>k</mi></mrow><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mn>0</mn></mrow></math></p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="ltx_p">Thus, choosing a subgroup <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\langle bK\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></math> of order <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p" display="inline"><mi>p</mi></math> in <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m10" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N(K)/K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></math>, let <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m11" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi:N(K)\to N(K)/K" display="inline"><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>K</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, sending <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m12" class="ltx_Math" alttext="g\mapsto gK" display="inline"><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
Constructing <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m13" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P=\pi^{-1}(\langle bK\rangle)" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><msup><mi>π</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m14" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ker\pi=K" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>ker</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mi>π</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow></math> and so <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p8.m15" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{P}\right|=\left|{P/K}\right|\left|{K}\right|=p(p^{k-1})=p^{k}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>K</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>K</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>p</mi><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>k</mi></msup></mrow></math>.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem7" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.3.7</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem7.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem7.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X=\left\{{P&lt;G\mid P\text{p-Sylow}}\right\},P\in X" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo lspace="0em">⁢</mo><mrow><mo fence="true" rspace="0em">&lt;</mo><mi>G</mi><mo fence="true" lspace="0em">∣</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0em">⁢</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mtext class="ltx_mathvariant_italic">p-Sylow</mtext></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
Then, <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem7.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X=G\cdot P=\left\{{gPg{-1}\mid g\in G}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p9" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Let <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p9.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S,P\in X" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi></mrow></math>.
We show that we can pick <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p9.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="a" display="inline"><mi>a</mi></math> s.t. <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p9.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="aSa^{-1}\subset P" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>S</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>⊂</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow></math> (since <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p9.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{S}\right|=\left|{P}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>S</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>P</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></math>).</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">We know <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline"><mi>S</mi></math> acts on <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G/P" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow></math>, with <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="s\cdot(gP)=(sg)P" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>g</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>g</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow></mrow></math>.
Then, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{(G/P)^{S}}\right|\equiv_{p}\left|{G/P}\right|\not\equiv_{p}0" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mi>S</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≢</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mn>0</mn></mrow></math>, so pick any <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="a\in(G/P)^{S}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mi>S</mi></msup></mrow></math>, so that for all <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="s" display="inline"><mi>s</mi></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="saP=aP" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>s</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>a</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, i.e. <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p10.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="a^{-1}Sa\subset P" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>⁢</mo><mi>S</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>a</mi></mrow><mo>⊂</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow></math>.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem8" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.3.8</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem8.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem8.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n_{p}" display="inline"><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></math> be the number of p-Sylow subgroups, and <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem8.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P" display="inline"><mi>P</mi></math> a p-Sylow group.
Then, <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem8.p1.m3" class="ltx_math_unparsed" alttext="n_{p}\mid\left|{G/P}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0.167em">∣</mo><mo fence="false" rspace="0.167em">|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>P</mi><mo fence="false">|</mo></mrow></math> and <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem8.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n_{p}\equiv_{p}1" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mn>1</mn></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Let <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math> be the set of p-Sylow subgroups, with <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> acting on <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math> by conjugation.
Then, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X=G\cdot P" display="inline"><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n_{p}=\left|{X}\right|=\left|{G\cdot P}\right|=\left|{G}\right|/\left|{G_{P}}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>P</mi></msub><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.
Since, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P&lt;G_{p}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p^{n}\mid G_{P}" display="inline"><mrow><msup><mi>p</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo>∣</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>P</mi></msub></mrow></math>, and so <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p11.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n_{p}\mid\left|{G}\right|/\left|{G_{P}}\right|\mid\left|{G/P}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo lspace="0em">⁢</mo><mrow><mo fence="true" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><msub><mi>G</mi><mi>P</mi></msub><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em">∣</mo></mrow><mo lspace="0em">⁢</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>/</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Moreover, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P&lt;G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math> acts on <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="X" display="inline"><mi>X</mi></math>, with <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{X}\right|\equiv_{p}\left|{X^{P}}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>P</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.
Charactizing <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{X^{P}}\right|" display="inline"><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>P</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow></math>, consider any <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S\in X^{P}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>∈</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>P</mi></msup></mrow></math>, so that <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\forall p\in P,pSp^{-1}=S" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo rspace="0.167em">∀</mo><mi>p</mi></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>P</mi></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>S</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>p</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>S</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, i.e. <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P&lt;N(S)" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.
Moreover, since <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P&lt;X^{P}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>P</mi></msup></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P" display="inline"><mi>P</mi></math> and <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m10" class="ltx_Math" alttext="S" display="inline"><mi>S</mi></math> are p-Sylow subgroups of <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m11" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N(S)" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math>, and thus, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m12" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P=nSn^{-1}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>S</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></mrow></math>.
Finally, since <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m13" class="ltx_Math" alttext="n\in N(S)" display="inline"><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>∈</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>S</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m14" class="ltx_Math" alttext="P=nSn^{-1}=S" display="inline"><mrow><mi>P</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>S</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>S</mi></mrow></math>, and <math id="Ch1.S3.SS1.p12.m15" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1=\left|{X^{P}}\right|\equiv_{p}\left|{X}\right|=n_{p}" display="inline"><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>|</mo><msup><mi>X</mi><mi>P</mi></msup><mo>|</mo></mrow><msub><mo>≡</mo><mi>p</mi></msub><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></mrow></math>.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section id="Ch1.S3.SS2" class="ltx_subsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">1.3.2 </span>Semi-Direct Products</h4>

<div id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Now that we have developed our key subgroups, we focus on how to compose them.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_definition">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Definition 1.3.9</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\triangleleft G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⊲</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="H&lt;G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="NH=G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math> and <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\cap H=\left\{{e}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>∩</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>e</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.
Then <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\rtimes H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋊</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math> is a group over the set <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\times H" display="inline"><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">×</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow></math> where <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem9.p1.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(n_{1},h_{1})(n_{2},h_{2})=(n_{1}(h_{1}n_{2}h_{1}^{-1}),h_{1}h_{2})" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Recall the similarities between the semi-direct product and the direct-sum from linear algebra.
The operation is forced in order for <math id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f:(n,h)\mapsto nh" display="inline"><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>h</mi></mrow></mrow></mrow></math> to be a homomorphism, since</p>
<table id="Ch1.Ex4" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_center"><math id="Ch1.Ex4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f(n_{1},h_{1})f(n_{2},h_{2})=(n_{1}h_{1})(n_{2}h_{2})=(n_{1}h_{1}n_{2}h_{1}^{-%
1})(h_{1}h_{2})=f((n_{1},h_{1})(n_{2},h_{2}))" display="block"><mrow><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msubsup><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msubsup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem10" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.3.10</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem10.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem10.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="N\rtimes H\cong G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋊</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>≅</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic"> (indeed is a group).</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">The identity element is <math id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(e_{N},e_{H})" display="inline"><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>N</mi></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>H</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></math>, where <math id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(n,h)(h^{-1}n^{-1},h^{-1})=(nhh^{-1}n^{-1},hh^{-1})=e" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>,</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><mi>h</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>e</mi></mrow></math>.
Moreover, the operation is associative,</p>
<table id="Ch3.S3.EGx1" class="ltx_equationgroup ltx_eqn_align ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody id="Ch1.Ex5"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_right ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch1.Ex5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle(n_{1},h_{1})((n_{2},h_{2})(n_{3},h_{3}))" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch1.Ex5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle=(n_{1},h_{1})(n_{2}(h_{2}\cdot n_{3}),h_{2}h_{3})" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
<tbody id="Ch1.Ex6"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch1.Ex6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle=(n_{1}(h_{1}\cdot(n_{2}(h_{2}\cdot n_{3}))),h_{1}h_{2}h_{3})" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
<tbody id="Ch1.Ex7"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch1.Ex7.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle=(n_{1}(h_{1}\cdot n_{2})(h_{1}h_{2}\cdot n_{3}),h_{1}h_{2}h_{3})" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>3</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
<tbody id="Ch1.Ex8"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch1.Ex8.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle=(n_{1}(h_{1}\cdot n_{2}),h_{1}h_{2})(n_{3},h_{3})" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
<tbody id="Ch1.Ex9"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch1.Ex9.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle=((n_{1},h_{1})(n_{2},h_{2}))(n_{3},h_{3})" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>n</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>h</mi><mn>3</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p4" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Finally, consider homomorphism <math id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\pi:N\rtimes H\to G" display="inline"><mrow><mi>π</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋊</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></mrow></math> sending <math id="Ch1.S3.SS2.p4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="(n,h)\mapsto nh" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>h</mi></mrow></mrow></math>, where</p>
<ul id="Ch1.S3.I2" class="ltx_itemize">
<li id="Ch1.S3.I2.i1" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.S3.I2.i1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Injective, since <math id="Ch1.S3.I2.i1.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ker\pi=\left\{{(n,h)\mid n=h^{-1}}\right\}\subset N\cap H=\left\{{e}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>ker</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mi>π</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo fence="true" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∣</mo><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>h</mi><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow><mo>⊂</mo><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>∩</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi>e</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow></mrow></math></p>
</div>
</li>
<li id="Ch1.S3.I2.i2" class="ltx_item" style="list-style-type:none;">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_item">•</span> 
<div id="Ch1.S3.I2.i2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Surjective, since <math id="Ch1.S3.I2.i2.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="NH=G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>H</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math></p>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
<p class="ltx_p">and so indeed, isomorphic.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section id="Ch1.S3.SS3" class="ltx_subsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">1.3.3 </span>Classification of Groups of order pq</h4>

<div id="Ch1.S3.SS3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">We conclude our chapter on group theory with a quick classification of some groups.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem11" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 1.3.11</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem11.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">If <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem11.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left|{G}\right|=p^{2}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo>|</mo><mi>G</mi><mo>|</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>p</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem11.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G\cong\mathbb{Z}_{p}\rtimes\mathbb{Z}_{p}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>≅</mo><mrow><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><mi>p</mi></msub><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋊</mo><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><mi>p</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></math> or <math id="Ch1.S3.Thmtheorem11.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G\cong\mathbb{Z}_{p^{2}}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>≅</mo><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><msup><mi>p</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></msub></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS3.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">If there is some <math id="Ch1.S3.SS3.p2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\langle g\rangle=G" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mi>g</mi><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch1.S3.SS3.p2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G\cong\mathbb{Z}_{p^{2}}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo>≅</mo><msub><mi>ℤ</mi><msup><mi>p</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></msub></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch1.S3.SS3.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Otherwise, consider <math id="Ch1.S3.SS3.p3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="G" display="inline"><mi>G</mi></math> acting on itself via conjugation.
