Now, pick adapted basis <math id="Ch3.S3.p2.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left\{{a_{1}w_{1},\ldots,a_{1}w_{k}}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mo>{</mo><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><mo>}</mo></mrow></math> and <math id="Ch3.S3.p2.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left\{{w_{1},\ldots,w_{m}}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mo>{</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo>}</mo></mrow></math> for <math id="Ch3.S3.p2.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\ker\phi" display="inline"><mrow><mi>ker</mi><mo lspace="0.167em">⁡</mo><mi>ϕ</mi></mrow></math> and <math id="Ch3.S3.p2.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M" display="inline"><mi>M</mi></math> respectively.
Finally, let</p>
<table id="Ch3.Ex4" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_center"><math id="Ch3.Ex4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T=\langle a_{1}w_{1}\rangle\oplus\ldots\oplus\langle a_{k}w_{k}\rangle\qquad F%
=\langle w_{k+1}\rangle\oplus\ldots\oplus\langle w_{m}\rangle" display="block"><mrow><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo>⊕</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>⊕</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mrow><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>k</mi></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>k</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mspace width="2em"></mspace><mrow><mi>F</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mrow><mi>k</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo>⊕</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>⊕</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>w</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p class="ltx_p">Then, <math id="Ch3.S3.p2.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T" display="inline"><mi>T</mi></math> torsion and <math id="Ch3.S3.p2.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="F" display="inline"><mi>F</mi></math> free, so they disjoint.
Moreover, they are generating (since form basis), so we win.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Uniqueness</span>:
Suppose <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M=T_{1}\oplus F_{1}=T_{2}\oplus F_{2}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⊕</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>⊕</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow></mrow></math>.
Then, <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T_{1}\subset M^{\text{tors}}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>⊂</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mtext>tors</mtext></msup></mrow></math>.
Moreover, for any <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m=t_{1}+f_{1}" display="inline"><mrow><mi>m</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>t</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow></mrow></math> torsion with <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="rm=0" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math>, <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="r\neq 0" display="inline"><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>≠</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="rt_{1}=-rf_{1}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>t</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo>−</mo><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="rf_{1}=0" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>r</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math> and <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f_{1}=0" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math>.
Thus, <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T_{1}=M^{\text{tors}}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mtext>tors</mtext></msup></mrow></math>, and similarly <math id="Ch3.S3.p3.m10" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T_{2}=M^{\text{tors}}=T_{1}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>T</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><msup><mi>M</mi><mtext>tors</mtext></msup><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>T</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.p4" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Now, consider <math id="Ch3.S3.p4.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\phi_{F_{i}}:M\to F_{i}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>ϕ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msub><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></math> surjective homomorphism, sending <math id="Ch3.S3.p4.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="t+f_{i}\mapsto f_{i}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>t</mi><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></math>.
Then, <math id="Ch3.S3.p4.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\phi_{F_{1}}=\phi_{F_{2}}=\text{id}-\phi_{T}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>ϕ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>ϕ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mtext>id</mtext><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>ϕ</mi><mi>T</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch3.S3.p4.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="F_{1}=\phi_{F_{1}}(M)=\phi_{F_{2}}(M)=F_{2}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>ϕ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>ϕ</mi><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></msub><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>M</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow></math>.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<section id="Ch3.S3.SS1" class="ltx_subsection">
<h4 class="ltx_title ltx_title_subsection">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_subsection">3.3.1 </span>Jordan Normal Form</h4>

<div id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">We can refine this theorem further.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem2" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 3.3.2</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">In a PID, <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\exists!\langle p_{1}\rangle,\ldots,\langle p_{m}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo rspace="0.167em">∃</mo><mo>!</mo></mrow><mo>⁡</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>m</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></math> (not necessarily distinct) irreducibles and <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem2.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="e_{1},\ldots,e_{m}&gt;0" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math> where</span></p>
<table id="Ch3.Ex5" class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_align_center"><math id="Ch3.Ex5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="M\cong R^{n}\oplus R/\langle p_{1}^{e_{1}}\rangle\cdots\oplus R/\langle p_{m}^%
{e_{m}}\rangle" display="block"><mrow><mi>M</mi><mo>≅</mo><mrow><msup><mi>R</mi><mi>n</mi></msup><mo>⊕</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn><msub><mi>e</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⋯</mi></mrow><mo>⊕</mo><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mi>m</mi><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p2" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">The free part is fixed.
Moreover, the torsion part is isomorphic to some <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p2.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="R/\langle a_{1}\rangle\oplus\cdots\oplus R/\langle a_{n}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>⊕</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⋯</mi><mo>⊕</mo><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mi>n</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.
Now, we may write each <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p2.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\langle a_{1}\rangle=\langle p_{1}^{e_{11}}\cdots p_{n}^{e_{1n}}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msub><mi>a</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><mrow><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn><msub><mi>e</mi><mn>11</mn></msub></msubsup><mo>⁢</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">⋯</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mi>n</mi><msub><mi>e</mi><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>⁢</mo><mi>n</mi></mrow></msub></msubsup></mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></math>, and applying the Chinese remainder theorem, we get existence.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Arguing uniqueness, we know the <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p_{i}" display="inline"><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></math> irreducibles are unique, since these are the terms in the ring for which there are zero vector-divisors (i.e. <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="pm=0" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>p</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>m</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mn>0</mn></mrow></math> for some <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="m\in M" display="inline"><mrow><mi>m</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>M</mi></mrow></math>).
Moreover, if <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\bigoplus_{i}R/\langle p_{i}^{e_{i}}\rangle\cong\bigoplus_{i}R/\langle p_{i}^{%
f_{i}}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><msub><mo>⨁</mo><mi>i</mi></msub><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow><mo rspace="0.111em">≅</mo><mrow><msub><mo>⨁</mo><mi>i</mi></msub><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, and ordering <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="e_{i}" display="inline"><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></math> and <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f_{i}" display="inline"><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></math> in ascending order, let <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\phi" display="inline"><mi>ϕ</mi></math> be the isomorphism.
Considering <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m8" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\phi^{\prime}=\phi\big{|}R/\langle p_{1}^{e_{1}}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><msup><mi>ϕ</mi><mo>′</mo></msup><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>ϕ</mi><mo fence="false" mathsize="1.200em">|</mo><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn><msub><mi>e</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m9" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\text{im }\phi^{\prime}=R/\langle p_{1}^{f_{1}}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mtext>im </mtext><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mi>ϕ</mi><mo>′</mo></msup></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>R</mi><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mn>1</mn><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, so <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p3.m10" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f_{1}=e_{1}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>e</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow></math> and we win via induction.
∎</p>
</div>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p4" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">With this form, we can derive the Jordan Normal Form.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3" class="ltx_theorem ltx_theorem_theorem">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_title_theorem">
<span class="ltx_tag ltx_tag_theorem"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">Theorem 3.3.3</span></span><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_bold">.</span>
</h6>
<div id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p"><span class="ltx_text ltx_font_italic">Let <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="V" display="inline"><mi>V</mi></math> be a <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathbb{C}" display="inline"><mi>ℂ</mi></math>-module and <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T:V\to V" display="inline"><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo lspace="0.278em" rspace="0.278em">:</mo><mrow><mi>V</mi><mo stretchy="false">→</mo><mi>V</mi></mrow></mrow></math> a linear transformation.
Then, <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="V" display="inline"><mi>V</mi></math> is a direct sum of generalized eigenspaces for <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T" display="inline"><mi>T</mi></math>, i.e. <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T(\beta_{i})=\lambda_{i}\beta_{i}+\beta_{i+1}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub></mrow></mrow></math> or <math id="Ch3.S3.Thmtheorem3.p1.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T(\beta_{i})=\lambda_{i}\beta_{i}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msub><mi>β</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></math>.</span></p>
</div>
</div>
<div class="ltx_proof">
<h6 class="ltx_title ltx_runin ltx_font_italic ltx_title_proof">Proof.</h6>
<div id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p5" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Consider <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p5.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="V" display="inline"><mi>V</mi></math> as a <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p5.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="C[x]" display="inline"><mrow><mi>C</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></mrow></math>-module, where <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p5.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="f\cdot v\mapsto f(T)(v)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>v</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>T</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, i.e. <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p5.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T(f\cdot v)=(xf)(T)(v)" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>v</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mi>f</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>T</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.
Write <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p5.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="V=\bigoplus\mathbb{C}[x]/\langle p_{i}^{e_{i}}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mi>V</mi><mo rspace="0.111em">=</mo><mrow><mo>⨁</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>ℂ</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">[</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">]</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>/</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msubsup><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msubsup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>.</p>
</div>
<div id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6" class="ltx_para">
<p class="ltx_p">Because <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\mathbb{C}" display="inline"><mi>ℂ</mi></math> is algebraically closed, <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="p_{i}=x-\lambda_{i}" display="inline"><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></mrow></math>.
Now, consider the basis <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m3" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\left\{{\ldots,(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}+\langle(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}}\rangle%
,\ldots}\right\}" display="inline"><mrow><mo>{</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>,</mo><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow><mo>,</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">…</mi><mo>}</mo></mrow></math>, for <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m4" class="ltx_Math" alttext="1\leq j\leq e_{i}" display="inline"><mrow><mn>1</mn><mo>≤</mo><mi>j</mi><mo>≤</mo><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow></math>.
Then,</p>
<table id="Ch3.S3.EGx3" class="ltx_equationgroup ltx_eqn_align ltx_eqn_table">

<tbody id="Ch3.Ex6"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_right ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch3.Ex6.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle T((x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}\cdot v)" display="inline"><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup><mo rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>v</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch3.Ex6.m2" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle\mapsto x\cdot(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
<tbody id="Ch3.Ex7"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch3.Ex7.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle\mapsto x\cdot(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}+\lambda(x-\lambda_{i})^{e%
_{i}}" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo lspace="0.222em" rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi>λ</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msup></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
<tbody id="Ch3.Ex8"><tr class="ltx_equation ltx_eqn_row ltx_align_baseline">
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padleft"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_eqn_cell"></td>
<td class="ltx_td ltx_align_left ltx_eqn_cell"><math id="Ch3.Ex8.m1" class="ltx_Math" alttext="\displaystyle=(x-\lambda_{i})(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}+\lambda(x-\lambda_{i})^%
{e_{i}-j}+\langle(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}}\rangle" display="inline"><mrow><mi></mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mrow><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mi>λ</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup></mrow><mo>+</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">⟨</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></msup><mo stretchy="false">⟩</mo></mrow></mrow></mrow></math></td>
<td class="ltx_eqn_cell ltx_eqn_center_padright"></td>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
<p class="ltx_p">Thus, for <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m5" class="ltx_Math" alttext="j&gt;1" display="inline"><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></math>, then <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m6" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T((x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}\cdot v)\mapsto(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-(j-1)}+%
\lambda_{i}(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-j}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup><mo rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>v</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>j</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow></msup><mo>+</mo><mrow><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>j</mi></mrow></msup></mrow></mrow></mrow></math>, and <math id="Ch3.S3.SS1.p6.m7" class="ltx_Math" alttext="T((x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-1}\cdot v)\mapsto\lambda(x-\lambda_{i})^{e_{i}-1}" display="inline"><mrow><mrow><mi>T</mi><mo>⁢</mo><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo rspace="0.055em" stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo rspace="0.222em">⋅</mo><mi>v</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></mrow><mo stretchy="false">↦</mo><mrow><mi>λ</mi><mo>⁢</mo><msup><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>−</mo><msub><mi>λ</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><msub><mi>e</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></mrow></mrow></math>.
∎</p>
